  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_1668d769-67b4-4efd-8b0f-117cbd0e10fc'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();

<span id="freeTextContainer3492732344172830191"><b>The legacy of the Black Dagger Brotherhood continues in a spin-off series from the #1 <i>New York Times</i> bestselling author…</b><br/><br/>Paradise, blooded daughter of the king’s First Advisor, is ready to break free from the restrictive life of an aristocratic female. Her strategy? Join the Black Dagger Brotherhood’s training center program and learn to fight for herself, think for herself</span>
  <span id="freeText3492732344172830191" style="display:none"><b>The legacy of the Black Dagger Brotherhood continues in a spin-off series from the #1 <i>New York Times</i> bestselling author…</b><br /><br />Paradise, blooded daughter of the king’s First Advisor, is ready to break free from the restrictive life of an aristocratic female. Her strategy? Join the Black Dagger Brotherhood’s training center program and learn to fight for herself, think for herself…be herself. It’s a good plan, until everything goes wrong. The schooling is unfathomably difficult, the other recruits feel more like enemies than allies, and it’s very clear that the Brother in charge, Butch O’Neal, a.k.a. the <i>Dhestroyer</i>, is having serious problems in his own life.<br /> <br />And that’s before she falls in love with a fellow classmate. Craeg, a common civilian, is nothing her father would ever want for her, but everything she could ask for in a male. As an act of violence threatens to tear apart the entire program, and the erotic pull between them grows irresistible, Paradise is tested in ways she never anticipated—and left wondering whether she’s strong enough to claim her own power…on the field, and off.</span>

<div id="review_1196696611" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1196696611" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1196696611?book_show_action=true">Feb 10, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

          marked it as to-read




        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=not-yet-released">not-yet-released</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=now">now</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1196696611" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer891093205350356401"><b> OMG!!! This is a new Black Dagger Brotherhood series focusing on the ORIGINAL brothers!!!!! We're talking Wrath, Rhage, Z., V., Butch, Tohr, Phury, Rehv, etc.</b><br/><br/><u>
  <i>Message from JR Ward</i>
</u>: I miss the Brothers. The original ones. We're talkin' the ones who started it all... Z., V., Butch, Rhage, Wrath, Tohr, Phury, Rehv, Etc.<br/><br/>I miss that scene, in DARK LOVER, when Fritz kindly asks the Brothers, if they're going to bloody the human, please take him outside.<br/><br/>I miss Sox hats and grey Goose, Tums and Toot</span>
  <span id="freeText891093205350356401" style="display:none"><b> OMG!!! This is a new Black Dagger Brotherhood series focusing on the ORIGINAL brothers!!!!! We're talking Wrath, Rhage, Z., V., Butch, Tohr, Phury, Rehv, etc.</b><br /><br /><u>
  <i>Message from JR Ward</i>
</u>: I miss the Brothers. The original ones. We're talkin' the ones who started it all... Z., V., Butch, Rhage, Wrath, Tohr, Phury, Rehv, Etc.<br /><br />I miss that scene, in DARK LOVER, when Fritz kindly asks the Brothers, if they're going to bloody the human, please take him outside.<br /><br />I miss Sox hats and grey Goose, Tums and Tootsie Rolls, Biggie Smalls in the Escalade, and Wrath putting a dagger into the wall next to Hollywood's head.<br /><br />As much as I LOVE the BDB series where it is now, and as much as I'm psyched to keep writing it and will continue to do so, I miss the good ol' days.<br /><br />The issue is that the nature of a series is that it must continue to grow, and change, or it dies. The Black Dagger Brotherhood books started off with the original Brothers, but after their meet-and-greets with their shellans were told, by definition, they had to background it in subsequent books: With a world as big as the BDB one, you have to train your "camera lens" in a controlled manner, or you run the risk of a given story bleeding out for too much extraneous stuff.<br /><br />(Something I've been tagged with doing from time to time, and it's certainly a fair point.)<br /><br />So when my boss (my editor) and I were chewing on things last spring, I told her... hey, I got this idea.<br /><br />I have a lot of ideas. She's used to this.<br /><br />I described to her a new series, where the BDB training center is reopened to a new cast of recruits, and THE ORIGINAL BROTHERS teach these FNUGs wassup. In the process of the new recruits falling in love and getting into a sh*t ton of trouble, THE ORIGINAL BROTHERS could be shown with their shellans, their Brothers, their people in the mansion, in a more prominent way than I'm able to do in the BDB books.<br /><br />Paperback, yo. Not hardcover. Traditional PNR, just like DARK LOVER was in the old days.<br /><br />Sex. Lot of sex. <br /><br />As in, you might need your BBQ tongs. Maybe a flame retardant suit. <br /><br />Maybe a fire truck on standby out in your front yard.<br /><br />My boss, who's brilliant, was like, wow, that really doesn't suck. (Okay, that's paraphrasing.)<br /><br />So... we have the first of the Black Dagger Legacy books, BLOOD KISS, coming out this December. <br /><br />Now, let me say this: the ORIGINAL BROTHERS are still going to show up in the BDB books. Hell, yeah! And from time to time, a BDB book is going to be about them and their mate if there's a big thing going on in their lives (think THE KING.) I am NOT taking a step away from the Brothers at all- if anything, I'm bringing them further to the forefront with the Black Dagger Legacy books.<br /><br />But I miss my boys :( I want to show you where they're at. I want to take you back to them- in their new roles as... well, role models and teachers. <br /><br />Before you ask, yes, they will still be colossal a&amp;&amp;holes- I mean, let's be clear. Things haven't changed THAT much. (As an aside, Doc Jess and I were talking the other day, and she was like, I'm so impressed with your ability to be offensive with your heroes. LOLOLOLOL)<br /><br />This is not to say that the Black Dagger Legacy books will solely be about the Brothers, however. The book will have a lot of the Brothers in them, but the Legacy books will feature a main romance between a couple, and the Brothers will help that along.<br /><br />eHarmony the BDB way.<br /><br />Jeez, I gotta be insane for signing up for this. Can you imagine V offering dating advice? "Well, sh*t, just get her some black candles and dog collar, true? Then order her to pop up her ***** **** * * ******* * * * ************** At that point, you're going to want to inform her, that you'll tell her when she can beg."<br /><br />Great. Really looking forward to this.<br /><br />*sigh*<br /><br />Anywho, the first Brother who's up?<br /><br />A certain cop. From Boston. Who's going to have his hands full with the new recruits- two of whom you'll meet in THE SHADOWS.<br /><br />A cover reveal is coming soon- but I couldn't sit on BLOOD KISS any longer!!!!<br /><br />Gahd, I suck at keeping secrets. But come on now, don't lie. You've missed those leathers, those sh*tkickers... that golf cart... the Pit.<br /><br />V nakey in the shower.<br /><br />Don't lie. <br /><br />I know I have!<br /><br />Happy Reading, and thank you for all your support, J.R.</span>
  <a data-text-id="891093205350356401" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</a><br/><br/><b>“Don’t put me on a pedestal. All I’ll do is fall from grace.”-Paradise</b><br/><br/>Blood Kiss is the first book in the spin-off series Black Dagger Legacy from the Black Dagger Brotherhood world.   <span id="freeText15585392076335032409" style="display:none"><b>4 Pedestal Stars </b><br> <br>First read 2015<br>Reread 4/18/2017<br><br><b>*Some Spoilers*</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/bo11_zpsjhrguy8n.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451246609ra/17520435.gif" alt=" photo bo11_zpsjhrguy8n.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“Don’t put me on a pedestal. All I’ll do is fall from grace.”-Paradise</b><br><br>Blood Kiss is the first book in the spin-off series Black Dagger Legacy from the Black Dagger Brotherhood world. In this series we meet the new trainees for the Brotherhood as well as check in and refall in love with couples from the BDB. This book is about Paradise and Craeg as well as Butch and Marissa. What I loved about this book is that it was just from the two couple's pov not a million other peoples pov like the last few BDB books have been. It really cuts down on the confusion and chaos of jumping from story line to story line and it felt more intimate. More like her earlier BDB books. <br><br><b>“Before you speak, be very aware that I love you. I love you with everything I have and all that I am. But if you do not get real with me, I’m going to go back to the Pit, pack a bag, and move to Safe Place for a while.” She held his stare with unwavering eyes. “You and I are not going to survive long term, regardless of love or bonding, if you keep airbrushing things. If I keep airbrushing things. It’s not a good strategy for us—and if this makes you feel like you’re on the spot? As if I’m giving you an ultimatum? I don’t care. If anything gets in the way of our relationship, anything, I will mow that shit down—even if it is you.”-Marissa </b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/Blood%20kiss_zpsqmfn87md.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451246609i/17520436._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Blood kiss_zpsqmfn87md.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“Do you like playing with fire, girl?” he growled. “Because if you keep looking at me like that, I’m going to burn you to the ground.”-Craeg</b><br><br>I felt the two couples complemented each other well as they were very much alike. Marissa and Paradise both are good girls, from good bloodlines, founding families, members of the glymera. Both don't like the restrictions of their births. Both fall in love with blue collar commoners. Both are sweet, brave and smart. Butch and Craeg are both common, poor hard working men. Both feel they are not good enough for the women they love. Both have dark past that effect who they are. Both are men of honor, and both are sexy as hell! I loved Craeg and Paradise together. They had great chemistry. I also really enjoyed getting reacquainted with Butch and Marissa. I loved that they are still very much in love with each other and that they seen the problems they had and worked on them. <br><br><b>“I can’t pretend to be sophisticated, or worldly about sex, but I know damn well that the need to diminish others when one is threatened is the mark of a coward, not a hero. Have a good rest of the night. I’ll see you tomorrow—if you decide to show up.”-Paradise</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/01347c36d85dd3639a9fef9569d6a145375a31f5f3e0603ffec42d243f5d8d6a_zpsfnbafzkw.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451246609i/17520437._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 01347c36d85dd3639a9fef9569d6a145375a31f5f3e0603ffec42d243f5d8d6a_zpsfnbafzkw.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“If I kiss you,” he growled, “there’s no going back. I might not fuck you right here, right now, but I’ll have you on your back the instant I get the goddamn chance.”-Craeg</b><br><br>I felt like both couples had the same underline problem which was the men putting the women on a pedestal. But I felt that both couples were sexy and sweet in their own right. I really liked the other trainees as well. Especially Novo and Axe. I can't wait to read their stories. I also can't wait to get some more of V and Doc Jane. The girls movie night part was so damn funny. I adored the girl bonding and thought it was too cute how the men freaked out over the girls watching Magic Mike XXL. Lassiter God Lassiter was funny as hell I really need Lassiter to get his own book, but truefully I have no clue who would make a good mate for him. I have to say I was a little sad that I didn't get any Z in this book as he is my favorite and I always want some Z, but over all I loved this book and can't wait for the next one to come out! Below I leave my favorite part of the whole book:<br><br><b>Wrath inhaled like he was about to break the news of a death in the family. “They’re having a movie night.” Butch rolled his eyes and went over to his chair. Yeah, it was a little weird to sit down without his Marissa by his side, but for crissakes, it was nothing to go Prozac over. Besides, he was glad his woman had friends in the house— “They’re watching Magic Mike,” someone said. “Is that a children’s show?” He sat back as Fritz put a heaping plate of lamb in front of him. “Thanks, man—oh, thanks, yeah, I’d love a drink. I’ll take a Lagavulin on the rocks—” Butch stopped talking as he realized the entire table of males was looking at him. “What?” “You haven’t heard about Magic Mike?” Rhage demanded. “No.” He leaned back again as his drink was delivered. “Thanks. Is it like Barney?” “It’s about strippers,” Hollywood countered. Butch frowned and lowered the glass from his lips. “I’m sorry?” V came in from the pantry with a thick pouch of tobacco, a pack of rolling papers, and a scowl like somebody had stripped his favorite sex toy of its batteries. “Naked,” Vishous muttered as he sat where Marissa should have been. “Buck-ass naked. And they’re humans. Christ, it’s like being shown up by a pack of dogs.” “In thongs,” someone else bitched. “Dogs in thongs.”-The brothers</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/anigif_enhanced-32388-1423016284-12-1435759483_zpswpc3qgat.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451246609ra/17520438.gif" alt=" photo anigif_enhanced-32388-1423016284-12-1435759483_zpswpc3qgat.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_1197094895" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1197094895" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1197094895?book_show_action=true">Feb 10, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1197094895" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17107276990390600450"><b>5 stars!</b> <br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/162ABB4E-43E5-4BF6-A6DD-C36A7A014885_zpsj8kukiji.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449499846i/17293218._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 162ABB4E-43E5-4BF6-A6DD-C36A7A014885_zpsj8kukiji.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>When I heard that a spin off book from the original BDB series I couldn’t contain my excitement. The BDB is one of my favorite series of all time. This book was amazing. It was one of the best BDB books I’ve read in a while. It felt like one of the original BDB books in the best way possible! <br/><br/>Over the last couple of books, we’ve met Paradise, an aristocratic daughter who’s father works for the King as his first advisor. Paradise has plans. She wants to join the BDB’s training progra</span>
  <span id="freeText17107276990390600450" style="display:none"><b>5 stars!</b> <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/162ABB4E-43E5-4BF6-A6DD-C36A7A014885_zpsj8kukiji.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449499846i/17293218._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 162ABB4E-43E5-4BF6-A6DD-C36A7A014885_zpsj8kukiji.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>When I heard that a spin off book from the original BDB series I couldn’t contain my excitement. The BDB is one of my favorite series of all time. This book was amazing. It was one of the best BDB books I’ve read in a while. It felt like one of the original BDB books in the best way possible! <br><br>Over the last couple of books, we’ve met Paradise, an aristocratic daughter who’s father works for the King as his first advisor. Paradise has plans. She wants to join the BDB’s training program and learn to fight for herself. Very few make the cut, and she is strong enough and determined enough to do it. She meets Craeg who is also in the training program. He’s in an entirely different class than Paradise. He’s from more of a working class and he’s lost his family to the raids. Could an aristocratic female fall in love with a civilian male? Even if he is the most worthy man she’s ever met, she knows it wouldn’t be approved by her father…<br><br>This book focuses on two couples (I was SO impressed how focused Ward was on just these two couples). The second is Butch and Marissa. Butch is one of the brothers who is leading the recruit program, and his mate, Marissa, runs Safe Place. There is a bit of a suspense in the plot that they’re connected to. I loved getting a new couple, then getting more of an older couple. It was a great balance. <br><br>Everything about this book was wonderful. Paradise is my new favorite female of the group. She’s strong, humble, and fearless. I loved how much humor was woven into the story. Lassiter is always good for laughs and the Magic Mike scene with the females cracked me up. For lovers of the BDB I can’t recommend this book enough! A full 5 stars from me!!!<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/7E589110-C402-415F-A054-2B336B55B293_zpsn5mdgncm.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449499846i/17293219._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 7E589110-C402-415F-A054-2B336B55B293_zpsn5mdgncm.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="17107276990390600450" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1197174478" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1197174478" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1197174478?book_show_action=true">Feb 10, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=pnr-vampires">pnr-vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=audio">audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1197174478" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11012229313127268149"><b>4 stars</b><br/><br/>I have been waiting such a long time for this book! The spin off to the Black Dagger Brotherhood series, JR Ward promised that this book would take us back to the original brothers, but also bring in some new blood by re-opening the training centre. And that’s exactly what we get - a bunch of new, young recruits with their very own hot romance, and a storyline for originals Butch and Marissa. Definitely a must-read for fans of the series, I wouldn’t recommend diving into this one without </span>
  <span id="freeText11012229313127268149" style="display:none"><b>4 stars</b><br /><br />I have been waiting such a long time for this book! The spin off to the Black Dagger Brotherhood series, JR Ward promised that this book would take us back to the original brothers, but also bring in some new blood by re-opening the training centre. And that’s exactly what we get - a bunch of new, young recruits with their very own hot romance, and a storyline for originals Butch and Marissa. Definitely a must-read for fans of the series, I wouldn’t recommend diving into this one without having read the BDB books first. <br /><br />Paradise has appeared in the last couple of books. She is the daughter of Wrath’s advisor, and a member of the glymera – the vampire elite - who dreams of more than the aristocratic life stretching out before her. When the Brotherhood re-open their training program, she signs up hoping to learn not only how to fight, but to discover who she is and what she wants from her life. <br /><br />Craeg joined the training program for a completely different reason. As a member of the vampire ‘blue collar’ class, he wants revenge on the people that he blames for the death of his family. He wants to become a warrior, and he will let nothing get in his way – not even his beautiful and tempting fellow trainee. <br /><br />Individually, I really liked Paradise and Craeg, but I didn’t feel their relationship as much as I usually do with the couples in this series. There wasn’t as much focus on them, and their relationship seemed based purely on their physical reaction to each other, and developed slowly with a start/stop thing as Craeg battled with his commitment to his training and his growing feelings for Paradise. And when they did interact, it wasn’t exactly deep and meaningful, but usually full of Craeg’s growly warnings to back off or lust-filled declarations.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Do you like playing with fire, girl?" he growled. Because if you keep looking at me like that, I'm going to burn you to the ground.”<br /><br />“If I kiss you,” he growled, “there's no going back. I might not fuck you right here, right now, but I'll have you on your back the instant I get the goddamn chance.”</i>
</blockquote><br />There’s no denying they were smoking hot together, but as for the actual ‘romance’…. yeah, not feeling it. But Paradise was the big surprise, and OMG, I love her! She’s a total badass! Not that’s she’s cold-hearted, she’s actually a real sweetheart, but she’s completely together, and emotionally strong and isn’t prepared to put up with any shit. She has been raised in the glymera with little expected of her but to mate well and look pretty, but damn, there’s so much to this girl! She struts into training with a ‘never quit’ attitude, and when Craeg starts jerking her around, she doesn’t let him get away with dismissing her and acting like an indecisive douche. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“This is getting us nowhere,” he muttered after a moment.<br />“You’re absolutely right. So fuck off. Have a nice life—hope all your holier-than-thou keeps you warm during the day.”</i>
</blockquote><br />The female is fantastic, and I have a total girl-crush on her!<br /><br />It was the other romance that felt like the main focus of the book, and which saved this book for me. I LOVED getting the chance to revisit with Butch and Marissa – their original story was fantastic, and I really enjoyed checking in with them again. They are still very much in love, but they have been together for a while now, and some issues are starting to appear. I thought it was very realistic considering who they are and everything they’ve been through, and I thought the way they dealt with it was fantastic! They didn’t hide from it, they worked on it, and they solidified their bond and fell even deeper in love with each other. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“I still think that every time I see you, after I’ve spent some time away from you. Thank God … he’s here.”</i>
</blockquote><br />Butch is a great character. His human past brings a wonderful dynamic to his character, and I liked that we got to see him still adjusting to that. But the big surprise with them was Marissa! The woman is a fierce!! She has really grown from the gentle, innocent aristocrat, and though she maintains that part of her, she’s also strong and passionate and not afraid to stand up to her man. She was so amazing in this book!<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“You and I are not going to survive long term, regardless of love or bonding, if you keep airbrushing things. If I keep airbrushing things. It’s not a good strategy for us—and if this makes you feel like you’re on the spot? As if I’m giving you an ultimatum? I don’t care. If anything gets in the way of our relationship, anything, I will mow that shit down—even if it is you.”</i>
</blockquote><br />The two relationships fit together really beautifully, with both couples having to sort through similar issues (and both females kicking ass!). Of course, they all get their HEA, but I have to admit that I was feeling it more for Butch and Marissa than I did with Paradise and Craeg. One storyline was so emotional, detailed and well-resolved, and the other was just…. not. But it all ended up in a good place, and I was happy with that. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>True love didn’t mean effortless, and ever-after wasn’t about cruise control. You started with the attraction, and then you opened your heart and your soul—but all that, which was no small thing, just got you to first base. There were many, many other trips to take to deeper levels of greater acceptance and understanding. That was where you found the happy. And the ever-after was the work you were always willing to put in to stay close, to learn, and to grow as people together.”</i>
</blockquote><br />Running alongside the romance is a murder/mystery storyline that I thought was really well done, and worked well as a catalyst for things that unfolded throughout the book. I liked the introduction we got to the other trainees, and am looking forward to seeing more of them in the future. And in exciting news, there are no lessers, no BoB, and the story is kept very much focussed on everything that happens between the two couples, with only their dual POVs telling the story. <br /><br />There were lots of light and funny moments. Any scene with Lassiter was great, but seeing the whole group of original characters was absolutely sensational! Butch and V together continue to be amazing – their teasing, slightly flirtatious friendship is both sweet and absolutely hilarious <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The whole “<i>I just fucked you in the ass</i>” conversation had me laughing out loud  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. The highlight for me was the scene where the girls all watched Magic Mike while the guys pathetically lamented their females looking at half naked humans. Freaking hilarious!<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>The hallway beyond was filled with males of the house, the Brothers and other fighters and Manny sitting on the floor with their backs to the bare walls, their legs stretched out, propped up, crossed at the knees or crossed at the ankles.<br />Apparently there had been quite a bit of drinking going on, bottles of vodka and whiskey littered around them, glasses in hands or on thighs.<br />“This is NOT as pathetic as it looks,” her Butch pointed out.<br />“Liar,” V muttered, “It so fucking is. I think I'm going to start knitting for reals.”</i>
</blockquote><br />God, I love these characters! I was so thrilled to be back in their world, and can’t wait for more.<br /><br />4 stars.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11012229313127268149" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1232986361" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1232986361" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8429172-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595453256p2/8429172.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1232986361?book_show_action=true">Mar 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/8429172-laura">Laura</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=oh-my-panties">oh-my-panties</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=until-the-end-of-the-world">until-the-end-of-the-world</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=jr-wards-world">jr-wards-world</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=fave-alpha-men">fave-alpha-men</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=amazing-heroines">amazing-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=girl-crush">girl-crush</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=ebooks-i-own">ebooks-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1232986361" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11570752670093825383"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420429845ra/13223235.gif' width='500' height='245' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>“I still think that every time I see you after I’ve spent some time away from you. ‘Thank God … he’s here.’”</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><b>Blurb:</b> Paradise, blooded daughter of the king’s First Advisor, is ready to break free from the restrictive life of an aristocratic female. Her strategy? Join the Black Dagger Brotherhood’s training center program and learn to fight for herself, think for herself…be herself. It’s a good plan, until everything goes wrong. And that’s before she falls in love with a fellow classmate. Craeg</span>
  <span id="freeText11570752670093825383" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420429845ra/13223235.gif" width="500" height="245" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“I still think that every time I see you after I’ve spent some time away from you. ‘Thank God … he’s here.’”</i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Blurb:</b> Paradise, blooded daughter of the king’s First Advisor, is ready to break free from the restrictive life of an aristocratic female. Her strategy? Join the Black Dagger Brotherhood’s training center program and learn to fight for herself, think for herself…be herself. It’s a good plan, until everything goes wrong. And that’s before she falls in love with a fellow classmate. Craeg, a common civilian, is nothing her father would ever want for her, but everything she could ask for in a male. As an act of violence threatens to tear apart the entire program, and the erotic pull between them grows irresistible, Paradise is tested in ways she never anticipated—and left wondering whether she’s strong enough to claim her own power…on the field, and off.<br><br>This is the best Ward has written in a long time. Guys, what a great time to be alive.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436290253ra/15443079.gif" width="500" height="232" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>BDB is really important to me—not only I’ve spent almost the last 10 years in company of the Brothers but it was my first PRN and Erotica encounter and it has brought me so much joy… but it’s not a surprise it kinda had lost its mojo and while I continue giving them a 5 stars rating and crying my eyes out, it’s not the same.<br><br>So, color me surprise when I started reading Blood Kiss and found kinda the same feeling I had while reading the first books. BDB earlier books were such a blast. They were funny, sexy, fast-paced, action packed and a lot of great things I’ve missed in the last books. I really <i>adored</i> this story. Was it perfect? No, but it was much needed.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/657699.gif" width="500" height="215" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Alright, this book follows to couples: Marissa/Butch and Craeg/Paradise.<br><br>Butch and Marissa are having some troubles communicating and they’re letting their previous lives get in the present and I think everything flew naturally. Like, we never expected their lives to be perfect all out of the blue and Butch was one of the Brothers who changed the most and I can’t begin to tell you how much Marissa’s life changed so this progression had to have some issues along the way and I was happy to see that.<br><br>Marissa is dealing with her broken relationship with his brother and all the years the glymera spent talking shit about her, putting her down and being downright assholes so when she found an almost dead girl outside Safe Place, she took things a bit too personal. The thing is, she didn’t deal with anything. She just swept it under the rug and tried to have her happy ever after.<br> <br>I never disliked Marissa even though I shipped V and Butch big time <s>I still kinda do</s> and while a lot of people found her boring, I appreciated her character a lot but this book? She totally rocked the fuck out of it. She has grown so much and we hadn’t seen it until now and I’m so proud of her. Not only she started to make amends and try find some peace but she stood in front of Butch and demanded things from him.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> “You and I are not going to survive long term, regardless of love or bonding, if you keep airbrushing things. If I keep airbrushing things. It’s not a good strategy for us—and if this makes you feel like you’re on the spot? As if I’m giving you an ultimatum? I don’t care. If anything gets in the way of our relationship, anything, I will mow that shit down—even if it is you.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441909012ra/16167132.gif" width="500" height="214" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Marissa has found a new voice and I just can’t wait to see more and more of her.<br><br>Now, with Butch things were totally different because while I never struggled with understanding what he wanted, I did not what the heck he was doing. I knew it had something to do with his dead sister, <i>since that wound never healed</i>, but I was afraid he was becoming an asshole. <br><br>Come on, he was doing to Marissa the same thing she escaped from and kinda belittling her. Granted, he just wanted the best for her but still. So, learning how he felt about his previous human life and his job as homicide detective and, like I said, transitions aren’t easy and while you can be happy you will still have some scars and that’s something I’m glad Ward showed.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448737741ra/17182144.gif" width="500" height="282" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Butch had Marissa on this pedestal and it wasn’t really fair to her but that’s because of his insecurities. I know Butch is waiting for the time when Marissa “realized she can do better” and while a little be of worry is healthy, it will not lead him to a good place. <br><br>And that deal with not letting Marissa suck him off? I was so sure it was going to be all about what the Omega did to him. Remember how he was after that in Lover Revealed? But his reason was unexpected and expected at the same time. I mean, we all know and love Butch but I’m happy he and Marissa talked about it and I’m happy he’s getting some closure about what happened to his sister and I know his relationship with Marissa will change for good.<br><br>Well, Paradise and Craeg were kinda tricky to swallow. Let me tell you why.<br>It’s not that I didn’t feel the connection between the two of them but everything happened in a really weird pace. <br><br>Sometimes it was fast, sometimes it was slow and I wasn’t really sure, towards the end of the book, if they were going to make it and I was <s>kinda</s> worried things were going to be left unsolved and then I had to wait for the next book and all of that so when things got solved, I can’t help to have this bittersweet feeling? Like, everything was rushed at the end and all that angst that was built during the whole book was fruitless? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1435255388ra/15322555.gif" width="500" height="254" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So that was really the only thing I didn’t like about the story because <b>I fucking loved Paradise.</b><br><br>Guys, I’m in love with this girl. I ain’t kidding.<br><br>I have such a crush on that woman and my respect for her was out of this world. Not only was she able to get into the training program  and kick ass  but she wanted something, err, someone, and she took it. It didn’t matter she was a virgin, it didn’t matter if she was an aristocrat, it didn’t matter what wasn’t relevant to her. She knows how the glymera operates and she wasn’t scared. <br><br>Gods, she was so sexy and she knew what she wanted.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424708509ra/13793943.gif" width="500" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b> With the grace of a dancer, she put her ass on the counter … then she drew her knees up and propped her high heels against the narrow walls of the alcove.<br>Giving him a stunning view of her black thigh-highs and her smooth, slick, bare sex.<br>“You know what I want,” she said. “And for once, it’s not your mouth there.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Paradise was so incredible cool, you have no idea how much I enjoyed reading her and how much I admired her. She was fearless in so many ways and she was decided type of girl who only wants her father to be proud of her and live her life on her own terms and you just can’t help but loving her. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/493623.gif" width="500" height="289" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She’s such a strong addition to the books and such a fresh female.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“This is getting us nowhere,” he muttered after a moment.<br>“You’re absolutely right. So fuck off. Have a nice life—hope all your holier-than-thou keeps you warm during the day.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Sometimes we overlook things for the people we love but that’s not healthy and I’m glad to read something like this.<br><br>Now, Craeg was difficult and while I sympathized with him in some ways, I couldn’t fall for him the way I wanted. <u>I fell for Paradise, as you can tell.</u> But I think he is going to be better as the books go, even though he won’t be a MC anymore, at least we’ll see some of his progress and that’ll be cool.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436290253ra/15443077.gif" width="500" height="281" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What happened to him and his family was horrible and reminded me of everything that happened with Lash and all the things we don’t see anymore on the BDB books.<br><br>As for the rest of the trainees, I can see the potential they all have and I’m really excited about Novo. <br><br>Here’s the thing: I’m so used to this shitty ass way some authors have to put woman against each other and so I was worried Novo, who was obviously built to that kind of training, was going to be a bitch to Paradise and she was going to see her as a threat but no. Gods, that was so not the case and I fucking loved it.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> “Lady and gentlemales,” Peyton said. “We have our Primus.”<br>“Don’t call me that,” she gritted before any kind of applause could happen. “Ever.”<br>“Why?” Novo challenged. “You beat all of us. You lasted the longest. You should be fucking proud of it.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436591893ra/15481843.gif" width="500" height="281" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She encouraged Paradise and she was downright great. I can’t wait to see more and more of her.<br><br>Which leads me to the motherfucking highlight of the book: <b>The women.</b><br><br>Ward redeemed herself on the thing I’ve always complained about her books and that’s the lack of female friendship. <br><br>Yes, they’re all friends but take and Mary and Bella. They were friends before they met Rhage and Z and after that? It was like the other didn’t exist. And yes, I know Ward’s prime focus if the Brothers but she needed to give the women more playground. <br><br>They’re all absolutely wonderful and so unique that the force they can be in the books… amazing and it was wasted and it’s like when people suddenly forget their friends because they now have a relationship and we all hate that so it was the same thing. And that only happened to girls.<br><br>Maybe it was Selana’s death that made Ward wake up and give the women the attention they deserved or I don’t know what it was but thank you. That chapter with the girl’s movie night and they being all wonderful to each other and having fun and the guys freaking out… I couldn’t stop laughing and it reminded me of the fun I used to have with the series and I’m glad we’re getting that back.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1421792732ra/13416353.gif" width="499" height="232" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now, what do I expect from this spin-off and from Ward in general?<br><br>• Bring the funny times back. We need to relax a little and she needs to get back to her roots.<br>• Since this book was a pretty cool start, I’m hoping as the story goes, the books get better and better.<br>• In the years to follow, and because she’s writing again about the original Brothers, I’m hoping she can bring back what we loved about them and also give them some closure already. I will miss having more books about them every year but I rather have them a fucking nice ending than prolong the story and have them vanish little by little and this Legacy spin-off it’s the perfect opportunity to do so.<br>• The Band of Bastards need to disappear. They worked while they were threat and that was for about two and half books. Now they do nothing but helping prolong a story that can only give so much.<br>• Assail, Luchas and the rest of the characters like that need to be grow up or die already.<br><br>So, overall Blood Kiss was a really good start with great female characters, a solid storyline and with all the potential of the world.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11570752670093825383" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1463367412" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5707032888998703254"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449590958ra/17309616.gif' alt=' photo giphy-4_zpslviueu7e.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>I’m thrilled and excited…………The Black Dagger Brotherhood world is back!!!!! <br/>Thank you…..<img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449590958i/17309617.jpg' alt=' photo 708e8afc82d6f57dd092f65bffa492c8_zpsdlexuct0.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Since the 1st book I read in your incredibly amazing BDB Series…..I have been hooked, addicted, obsessed, possessed, passionate…damn…..there are not enough words to describe how much I feel about the world and characters that you have created…………..you now have a fan in me for life…..<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449590958ra/17309618.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_m3v37ea9kL1r7krif_zpsqbbbgp9m.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Why did I ever doubt that you would be able to continue that BDB magic?<br/><br/>Okay, let me just write down my thoughts and feelings abo</span>
  <span id="freeText5707032888998703254" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449590958ra/17309616.gif" alt=" photo giphy-4_zpslviueu7e.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I’m thrilled and excited…………The Black Dagger Brotherhood world is back!!!!! <br>Thank you…..<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449590958i/17309617.jpg" alt=" photo 708e8afc82d6f57dd092f65bffa492c8_zpsdlexuct0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Since the 1st book I read in your incredibly amazing BDB Series…..I have been hooked, addicted, obsessed, possessed, passionate…damn…..there are not enough words to describe how much I feel about the world and characters that you have created…………..you now have a fan in me for life…..<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449590958ra/17309618.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m3v37ea9kL1r7krif_zpsqbbbgp9m.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Why did I ever doubt that you would be able to continue that BDB magic?<br><br>Okay, let me just write down my thoughts and feelings about Blood Kiss, the 1st book in the Black Dagger Legacy Series, the spinoff of the original BDB Series.<br><br>I’m not going into the storyline here….by now, all the BDB fans and others know it….so, let’s get to what I loved about the story.<br><br> What a brilliant move! Not only do we connect with the brothers and their shellans that we have come to adore – bonus…. but we are now introduced to the new warrior recruits wanting to join the BIG TEAM!!! <br><br>And even when we have glimpses of past favorites, the storyline is told by only 4 different POV’s……..Craeg &amp; Paradise (new recruits) and Butch and Marissa!! The focus is on these two couples which is really great….giving the readers an in depth look into these characters and their relationships.<br><br>The first couple….Craeg and Paradise, were really sweet and endearing. Paradise, glymera royalty, daughter of Wrath’s First Advisor and Craeg, a commoner. When the two meet during their training, more than sparks fly. Both feel a deep connection with each other and Craeg tries to fight his feelings for her because he believes he’s not good enough for someone like her. But Paradise wants more from the life that has been mapped out for her….<blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449590958i/17309619.jpg" alt=" photo 462e62dc66237125da40cd2498205f1e_zpsnxpazaob.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote><br>The more Craeg fights the feelings he has for Paradise, the more she pushes him…..I loved that their relationship wasn’t one of those insta-love things…..it grew with time and with both struggling to overcome the obstacles that faced them….<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449590958i/17309620.jpg" alt=" photo Kissing-couple-portrait.1-440x294_zpswsllq3hy.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I adored Paradise…never mind that I thought her name was a bit “naff”…..she had strength and determination to do something worthwhile with her life, she had focus, and she was caring and looked out for the underdog. I loved her grit, willpower and her purpose to wanting something more than just being a spoilt and cosseted member of the glymera.<br>And the fact that she was not afraid to kick Craeg’s butt…….when he continued with his “I’m not good enough for you” shit….you go girl!!<br><blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449590958i/17309621.jpg" alt=" photo unnamed_zpsfaytjyvj.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote>I liked these two as a couple. I found them very engaging and endearing…..although…yes, there is one of those…..I wanted a bit more zing, more heat when they gave in to those emotions…you know what I mean….okay, the encounters were a bit….let’s just said…I wanted to feel the HEAT we have become familiar with of the BDB couples. Nevertheless, I enjoyed their moments together….<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449590958ra/17309622.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lvujq3NDkd1qcxrpgo1_500_zpsqxwar8ek.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Now, onto Butch and Marissa…….<br>Butch is still a lovable character…still loves his designer wardrobe, which he doesn’t mind sharing with Craeg, who doesn’t have a wardrobe at all!!! He still kicks ass. He continues his connection and funny interaction with Vishous and he’s still totally over everything in love with his princess…Marissa. He still sees her as this Madonna…..in that high pedestal. <br>Their relationship is still strong but there are a few cracks that show up here. Their love for each other is really beautiful….<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449590958i/17309623.jpg" alt=" photo c6fca27971c2a726461591737c6fb991_zpsjtofac7a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Marissa has truly grown and become a really strong person. She wants Butch to see the real her instead of the person he’s placed on a pedestal. I grew to love her even more….how she dealt with her estranged brother, Havers, how she dealt with the death of an unknown woman in the Safe House and how she’s coming out of her repressed shell….<br><br>My all time favorite scene in this book………the girls night….what a time the shellans had together watching…..yes, wait for it…MAGIC MIKE XX3<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449590958ra/17309624.gif" alt=" photo magic-mike-5_zpsncdqqp4c.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And the guys waiting outside the room……..discussing what the girls were doing? I was rolling on the floor…laughing my head off….<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449590958ra/17309625.gif" alt=" photo 61ed924805553bfc2f5a7c6350128db8_zpstqm49gsv.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Oh, that’s Butch chasing Marissa after the movie!!!!<br>Loved the 1st training exercise that the brothers devised for the new recruits!!! Whew….action, unexpected surprises…..totally wicked….and of course Lassiter had a part in it too…<br><blockquote>I love this angel!!! Please can we get his story SOON?????<br><br>The mystery serial killer subplot??? Yeah….a bit weak!!!! That’s probably the only “peeve” I have!!!<br><br>I so liked this book…….and I can’t wait for some more!!!<br><br>SOON!!!!!</blockquote></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1448481771" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1448481771" />
    <a title="Jen Davis" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4669344-jen-davis"><img alt="Jen Davis" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1548427639p2/4669344.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1448481771?book_show_action=true">Nov 21, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen Davis" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen Davis" href="/user/show/4669344-jen-davis">Jen Davis</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1448481771" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer947448519471270415"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br/>This is the best Black Dagger Brotherhood book I've read in years. I've struggled with some of the later books in the series, as JR Ward started including too many secondary storylines in each installment. There were so many threads happening in each book, it detracted from the main romance, which ended up rather lackluster as a result. Not here. Yes, there is a secondary storyline. One. And it ended up merging with primary story quite organically. I didn't get bored. I didn't want to s</span>
  <span id="freeText947448519471270415" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br />This is the best Black Dagger Brotherhood book I've read in years. I've struggled with some of the later books in the series, as JR Ward started including too many secondary storylines in each installment. There were so many threads happening in each book, it detracted from the main romance, which ended up rather lackluster as a result. Not here. Yes, there is a secondary storyline. One. And it ended up merging with primary story quite organically. I didn't get bored. I didn't want to skip anything. And both main characters made it alive to the end of the book. Progress.<br /><br />If you've been away from the BDB books for a while and you are wondering if you can jump in here, the answer is an unresounding yes. You only need to be aware of the basics in the Marissa/ Butch/ V relationship. That, and the fact that the hero and heroine met once before, as he asked her for an application to join the Brotherhood and she gave it to him. Now you're ready.<br /><br />The whole premise of this quasi-spinoff is that the Brotherhood is opening its doors to trainees. The core romances will circle around these new characters. But this didn’t feel like a spinoff because it’s steeped deep in the core characters from the early original books. Especially Butch and Vishous. But almost everyone is there from Wrath to Rhage, even Bella and Z.<br /><br />But as promised, our main couple consists of two members of the training class. Paradise (whose name may be the worst thing in the book) is the daughter of Wrath’s First Advisor. She is pure pedigree glymera, but she wants more from her life than to be a cosseted child, with no rights or choices. Craeg is a working class vampire, who has joined the training program after the deaths of his family. He is attracted to Paradise from the beginning, but fights it. Obviously, it’s a fight he loses, but it’s fun watching him fall.<br /><br />A lot of time is spent with Butch and Marissa, who are a good parallel for Craeg and Paradise. The major themes in the book include the elitism of vampire culture and way the glymera treats its women. Marissa is still struggling with how that affected her past as Wrath’s betrothed and how it led to her break with her brother, Havers. Add to that, Butch’s tendency to put her on a pedestal and she has some stuff to work through, especially when a battered young woman lands on her safe house doorstep, and she has to turn to Havers for help.<br /><br />I really liked Paradise as a heroine. She is strong and takes control of her life in a society where that is very difficult for a female to do. She goes after what she wants, while still maintaining her empathy and humility. Craeg is sexy and strong, but in a lot of ways, has more growing to do than Paradise does. I liked the tension between them and thought they were a good match, despite the differences in their history.<br /><br />My only niggle: I thought the bad guy was pretty obvious from early on. You’ll figure it out long before the big reveal. But it didn’t really detract from my enjoyment of the story. I will definitely keep reading for the next installment. I’m curious which recruit will be up next.<br /><br />Rating: B+/A-<br /><br /><i>*ARC provided by publisher</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="947448519471270415" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1449158539" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1449158539" />
    <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance"><img alt="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1376622739p2/5498948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1449158539?book_show_action=true">Nov 22, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance">Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1449158539" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17847084651286598851"><b>3.5- 4 Stars</b><br/><img src='https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448905736r/17204777.jpg?144890573630998' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png' width='50' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>Do you like playing with fire, girl?" he growled. Because if you keep looking at me like that, I'm going to burn you to the ground."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448909655ra/17205212.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>The BDB series is sentimental for me. It's <b>the</b> series that got me into reading in the first place. It began what was to become what I refer to as my <b> PNR binge of 2009</b>. I was obsessed with that series...until I hit book 6. Then it slowly but surely began to lose some of its luster for me. By book 11 I had given up. It became too muddied with </span>
  <span id="freeText17847084651286598851" style="display:none"><b>3.5- 4 Stars</b><br><img src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448905736r/17204777.jpg?144890573630998" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Do you like playing with fire, girl?" he growled. Because if you keep looking at me like that, I'm going to burn you to the ground."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448909655ra/17205212.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The BDB series is sentimental for me. It's <b>the</b> series that got me into reading in the first place. It began what was to become what I refer to as my <b> PNR binge of 2009</b>. I was obsessed with that series...until I hit book 6. Then it slowly but surely began to lose some of its luster for me. By book 11 I had given up. It became too muddied with too many secondary POVs that the romance began to wane in the background. I missed the original brothers, the romance, the true BDB, true? So when I heard that JR Ward plans to come out with a new series that will be back to what the first few BDB books started off as with the original brothers; Wrath, Z, Butch, V, Rhage? Well, let's just say I knew I'd part with an ovary to get my grubby little hands on it.<br><br>I'll start my review by answering two questions first:<br><b>Is Blood Kiss like the BDB used to be?</b><br><i>Almost. It was probably the best Ward book I've read since book 8, and that's saying a lot. </i><br><b>Is this a true spin off?</b><br><i>Yes and no. Black Dagger Legacy focuses on a whole new slew of characters in the form of BDB trainees. But all the original brothers are also front and center. While the author does a good sum-up of important details, readers that haven't read the BDB series (or at least the first 5 books) would not enjoy it as much. It's set heavily in the BDB world, and you don't get much detail about the world building. The original BDB is what sets that up, so I highly recommend reading that first. So let's call it a quasi spin-off.</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448911405ra/17205436.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Blood Kiss follows two couple story lines; Butch and Marissa and Paradise and Craeg. I'd estimate it to be about 60/40 with no additional POVs to be found. Just the four. I'll give you a moment to contain your shock...<br>The two story lines run flawlessly together and drive the story line for the other. I, of course would never complain about getting more Butch considering he's one of my favorite brothers.<br><br>Paradise is a fully blooded daughter of the king's First Advisor who also happens to be one of the Founding Families of the glymera. She's expected to follow the protocol of the females of the glymera, but she wants nothing to do with it. Instead, she joins the BDB training program, to learn how to protect herself and her race. While growing up sheltered in the aristocratic society, I was happy to see that Paradise wasn't the stuffy, formally speaking heroine I anticipated her to be. She knows her own mind and while she may be sheltered on some things, she can kick some ass in her own right. And she definitely proves that when she's tested to her limits in the rigorous and and intense training program. Her one distraction comes in the form of the one male that should be hands off for her; a civilian.<br><br>Craeg is a nobody that came from nothing. After a brutal tragedy leaves him with nothing but thoughts of ahvenging it, he joins the BDB training program. Having handed his application to Paradise when first applying, he thinks that she's just a simple secretary. But he still knows that he's not good enough for the likes of her. He has nothing to offer and so no matter how enticing the female may be, he does his damnedest to push her away...even as he lusts for her at the same time.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">If I kiss you," he growled, "there's no going back. I might not fuck you right here, right now, but I'll have you on your back the instant I get the goddamn chance."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>In the midst of this story line you get Butch and Marissa who are dealing with issues of their own. Butch continues to put Marissa on a pedestal that she doesn't want to be on. After the glymera turned her back on her, her sole focus has been the Safe Place and her hellren. But there's a piece of Butch that he's still keeping hidden from her and she's determined to find out what that is. <br><br>I absolutely loved getting more Marissa and Butch. Their story line felt like a natural progression of their relationship without feeling like drama was being contrived. Butch's issues and Marissa's unresolved feelings with her estranged brother were bound to hit, and they hit here. I think I liked Marissa even more in this book than I did in her own. She truly grew into her own and became a strong heroine. As for Butch? What can I say about my favorite Southie? The man never fails to get my ovaries to flutter.<br><br>I have to admit I was a lot more invested in the developing storyline between Marissa and Butch than I was with Paradise and Craeg. Paradise and Craig's relationship was a tad too stretched out for my particular tastes and I was just itching for them both to get on with things. That being said, I did like them as individual characters. They just didn't quite have the intensity as a couple as some of the original BDB ones did for me. That's not to say it was bad, but I'd say that Marissa and Butch were the glue that held the story together.<br><br>The suspense story line came in the shape of a bad guy that wasn't a lesser for once. Admittedly I was a bit underwhelmed by this as well, as I had figured out who it was pretty early in the story. It was a bit too predictable and I wished for a little bit more on that end. I also didn't quite form a connection to any of the secondary characters that were introduced as new trainees here. They all had their uniqueness but none drew me like the original brothers did. But then again, it is hard to live up to the greatness that was the first 5 books so I may be judging unfairly.<br><br>I was happy to have a book with just four solid POVs that finally felt like the PNR it started out as originally. While it didn't quite blow me away, it was a great beginning to a series that I'm hoping will stay with the same formula and get even better with the next installment.<br><br><i>ARC courtesy of publisher in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br><b>Find me on:<br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/DirtyGirlRomance?" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436986543i/15525717.png" width="40" height="40" alt="Follow me on facebook" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a href="https://twitter.com/DirtyGrlRomance" target="twitter" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436986543i/15525718.png" width="40" height="40" alt="Follow Me on Twitter" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a href="http://www.dirtygirlromance.com" target="blog" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436986543i/15525719.png" width="40" height="40" alt="blog" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><a href="http://dirtygirlromance.com" target="blog" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436477285i/15465455._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="17847084651286598851" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6603203-pavlina-read-more-sleep-less-blog?shelf=want-to-read-soon">want-to-read-soon</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1196946073" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2168819508882461353"><br/> <b>4.5 BRILLIANT STARS</b><br/><br/>What an amazing story! It had everything I was expecting and more! J.R. Ward proved once again what a talented author she is! I was super excited about this one, it was one of my most anticipated books for December. I loved the story and I liked how it developed with half of the book about Marissa and Butch, if you have read the other books from BDB you already know Marissa and Butch. And the other half centered on Craeg and Paradise! This story was captivating, funny, myster</span>
  <span id="freeText2168819508882461353" style="display:none"><br> <b>4.5 BRILLIANT STARS</b><br><br>What an amazing story! It had everything I was expecting and more! J.R. Ward proved once again what a talented author she is! I was super excited about this one, it was one of my most anticipated books for December. I loved the story and I liked how it developed with half of the book about Marissa and Butch, if you have read the other books from BDB you already know Marissa and Butch. And the other half centered on Craeg and Paradise! This story was captivating, funny, mysterious and hot! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449254720ra/17257109.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I liked Craeg and Paradise, I felt their chemistry and I enjoyed how their relationship was progressed. There was palpable tension between them and it made their story that much more interesting. Paradise is an amazing heroine. She is strong and I liked that she takes the control of her life. Also, she isn’t afraid to show how she feels. Craeg is super hot and strong. <br><br><b>“I shouldn’t be touching you like this,” he said softly. No, she thought. He shouldn’t. “Don’t stop.” His head angled up, and his eyes met hers. “This is not a good idea.”</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449254720ra/17257110.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Marissa and Butch weren’t one of my favorite couples but I like that they were included in this one, and I can say that, I now feel more connected to them. <br><br>Overall the story is refreshing! It felt like the first time I read a book by this author! If you are a fan of J.R. Ward you know how brilliant her stories are!</span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="❤️ Dorsey aka Wrath Lover Reviews ❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="❤️ Dorsey aka Wrath Lover Reviews ❤️" href="/user/show/5205999-dorsey-aka-wrath-lover-reviews">❤️ Dorsey aka Wrath Lover Reviews ❤️</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/26823112-blood-kiss">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5205999-dorsey-aka-wrath-lover-reviews?shelf=jr_ward">jr_ward</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5205999-dorsey-aka-wrath-lover-reviews?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5205999-dorsey-aka-wrath-lover-reviews?shelf=audio_books">audio_books</a>
