    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1197843169" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13628582857665399305"><b>3/06/16</b><br/>Rereading just because I need a J.R. Ward fix!!!! 29 more days till we get <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25293695.The_Beast__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___14_' title='The Beast (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #14) by J.R. Ward' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Beast</a>!!!!! <br/><br/>* Just as awesome the second time around!!!!<br/><br/><br/><b>Originally read & reviewed: Dec 2015</b><br/><br/>Blog post: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.sweptawaybyromance.com/2015/12/blood-kiss-black-dagger-legacy-1-by-jr.html'>http://www.sweptawaybyromance.com/201...</a><br/><br/><b>
  <i>5 Classic BDB Stars!!!!</i>
</b><br/><br/>I'll start by saying that I'm a <b>
  <i>devoted BDB die-hard fangirl</i>
</b> and I have loved each and every BDB book, obviously some more than others but nevertheless I love them all!! I was extremely excited when I heard that The WARDen was writing a spin</span>
  <span id="freeText13628582857665399305" style="display:none"><b>3/06/16</b><br>Rereading just because I need a J.R. Ward fix!!!! 29 more days till we get <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25293695.The_Beast__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___14_" title="The Beast (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #14) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">The Beast</a>!!!!! <br><br>* Just as awesome the second time around!!!!<br><br><br><b>Originally read &amp; reviewed: Dec 2015</b><br><br>Blog post: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.sweptawaybyromance.com/2015/12/blood-kiss-black-dagger-legacy-1-by-jr.html">http://www.sweptawaybyromance.com/201...</a><br><br><b>
  <i>5 Classic BDB Stars!!!!</i>
</b><br><br>I'll start by saying that I'm a <b>
  <i>devoted BDB die-hard fangirl</i>
</b> and I have loved each and every BDB book, obviously some more than others but nevertheless I love them all!! I was extremely excited when I heard that The WARDen was writing a spin off series that will have more of the original brothers featured as the Brotherhood will be re-opening the Training Center to anyone (commoner, civilian, or aristocrat) and the Brothers would be front and center!! The initial test of endurance was intense!! Out of sixty candidates, only seven make it through, and they are a very diverse set of potential fighters. These seven will begin their training to fight, in the ongoing war...<i>but</i> I'm thinking there will be more to their roles because of the circumstances surrounding the Butch/Marissa story line and the investigation...we shall see.<br><br>This first book in the BDB Legacy Series <b>
  <i>Blood Kiss</i>
</b> focuses on two couples: Butch &amp; Marissa and Craeg &amp; Paradise and, the similarities between these couples, was not lost on me. In Blood Kiss, Paradise, is from one of the founding families of the Glymera and is the daughter of Abalone, First Adviser to The King. She's expected to follow protocol that all blooded daughters of the Glymera follow, however, she wants nothing to do with it. Instead she desperately desires to join the training program, she wants to learn how to protect herself and her race. While growing up she was sheltered by her beloved father but she is far from a stuck up Glymera socialite, she's definitely not the heroine I was expecting. She knows her own mind, shes determined, stubborn and, she knows what she wants and isn't afraid to go after it, she is definitely one determined young lady!! Best of all, she can kick ass, she proves it during the <i>extremely intense</i> training program. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Do you like playing with fire, girl?" he growled. Because if you keep looking at me like that, I'm going to burn you to the ground." ~Craeg</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Her one distraction is Craeg, they have an very intense attraction and are definitely aware of one another. Craeg is a “commoner” and after a brutal tragedy his main focus is the desire to avenge the deaths of his family, so he joins the BDB training program. Having first come into contact with Paradise as the receptionist at the Kings Audience House when he picked up an application to enter the training program and he believes she's a commoner too while Paradise keeps her status to herself not wanting to be looked at differently.<br> <br><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/Book%20Review%20Photos/PicsArt_1449118472210_zpsaawr3ubd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449267333i/17258144.jpg" alt=" photo PicsArt_1449118472210_zpsaawr3ubd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>If I kiss you," he growled, "there's no going back. I might not fuck you right here, right now, but I'll have you on your back the instant I get the goddamn chance." ~Craeg</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>We get a look into the relationship between Butch and Marissa. Butch and Marissa love each other, but their relationship is put to the test when a girl is brutally assaulted and ends up at Safe Place in Marissa’s care. Marissa is still struggling with things from her past involving her failed betrothal to Wrath and her brother Havers setting her out, along with Butch’s tendency to put her on a pedestal therefore not treating her as a true partner and confiding in her.<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“You and I are not going to survive long term, regardless of love or bonding, if you keep airbrushing things. If I keep airbrushing things. It’s not a good strategy for us, and if this makes you feel like you’re on the spot? As if I’m giving you an ultimatum? I don’t care. If anything gets in the way of our relationship, anything, I will mow that shit down, even if it is you.” ~ Marissa to Butch</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br><br><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/Book%20Review%20Photos/PicsArt_1449032229249_zpsdzhdmeeg.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449267333i/17258145.jpg" alt=" photo PicsArt_1449032229249_zpsdzhdmeeg.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I would have loved more time with Craeg and Paradise, but I loved Butch and Marissa's story too and I can't wait to see which trainee will be featured in the next Legacy book! I'm so happy that we are given a glimpse into our original beloved BDB characters. We get alittle everyone from Wrath to Rhage, V, Mary, Manny, Bella, Nalla, Z and our favorite (halirous) Fallen Angel Lassiter, Now I have to wait till <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25293695.The_Beast__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___14_" title="The Beast (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #14) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">The Beast</a> released in April 2016 for more of my beloved BDD. <br><br><u>
  <b><i>One</i> of my Favorite Scenes:</b>
</u><br>Girl's night for the mated women watching "Magic Mike" in the compounds theater. The bonded vampires are <i>extremely possessive</i> of their females and just the thought of them watching a stripper movie with sexy men......<i>very</i> entertaining!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="13628582857665399305" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1196694418" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1196694418" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1196694418?book_show_action=true">Feb 10, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25144725-blood-kiss">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1196694418" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16910984060232968402">Blood Kiss is a story about some new recruits in the training center that the Brotherhood is putting on. It's also a story that focuses on Butch and Marissa's relationship. There's also a murder and believe it or not, JRW works her magic and manages to twist the story lines together and bring it to a satisfying conclusion. <br/><br/>Since this is supposed to be a spin off series, let's talk about that for a minute. There's really not much differences from the prior books. The one thing that is missing is </span>
  <span id="freeText16910984060232968402" style="display:none">Blood Kiss is a story about some new recruits in the training center that the Brotherhood is putting on. It's also a story that focuses on Butch and Marissa's relationship. There's also a murder and believe it or not, JRW works her magic and manages to twist the story lines together and bring it to a satisfying conclusion. <br><br>Since this is supposed to be a spin off series, let's talk about that for a minute. There's really not much differences from the prior books. The one thing that is missing is all the POVs which was a much needed change, as well as, some fresh "blood". JRW gets to dwell on only two different couples, one new and one old, and give us some interesting insights. <br><br>Now for the problems...I'm not a big fan of Butch and Marissa as a couple so I wasn't too excited for more of their story. But I do like Butch so I was interested in seeing where JRW would go with him. It was okay...maybe some unnecessary drama but drama that brought them closer together. And the big problem for me was that their story took away from Paradise and Craeg who I <i>really</i> liked. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444367880ra/16491381.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So Paradise and Craeg....a much younger couple who for the most part didn't know what in the hell they were doing! I mean, don't they know anything about the bonding scent and the possessiveness? Obviously not! But I loved how they couldn't resist each other...I just hated that it took so long for things to happen and then <b>*boom*</b> the book was over. <br><br>One of the funniest scenes was when the girls got together for movie night....and the movie just happened to be <i>Magic Mike XXL</i>! It was hilarious...those poor bastards! and yes, my opinion of them did change...not sure if that's a good thing! ;) But what was up with all the not naming names? "Somebody yelled this" and "somebody said that"...I think it would have been better saying who said what! <br><br>And I loved getting little scenes with several of the older characters although I missed Wrath! :( Lassiter was a blast though but I was definitely left wanting more Rhage and JM! <br><br>I wasn't really impressed with the new recruits either except for Paradise and Craeg, what a band of misfits! Oh well, I guess it will just make things interesting. <br><br>Of course, there's nothing about who the next book will be about but I'm guessing either Peyton or Novo or Peyton <i>and</i> Novo. And as far as the prior couples go...Rhage and Mary should be out since the next book is about them and Wrath and Beth just had a book. That leaves a whole lotta other couples it could be but I'm thinking we need a V and Jane fix, true? <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450851590i/17477600.png" width="400" height="125" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quote:</u>
</b><br><br>♥ “Anywhere you take me, tonight and always.”<br><br><br><i>(Prior to review...)</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385488827ra/7160268.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>ETA:</b> I'm more excited to read this book after reading <i>The shAdoWs</i>!</span>

<div id="review_1428985897" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1428985897" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1428985897?book_show_action=true">Oct 30, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=5-stars-favorites">5-stars-favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1428985897" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14385956987733579461"><b>5 Recruit me Stars</b><br/><br/>I love JR WARD and I love the Black Dagger Brotherhood (BDB) series. Blood Kiss is a spin-off from the BDB series. You do not need to read the BDB books, however you get the full effect if you do. Blood Kiss is part of the Black Dagger Legacy. These books will focus on the new recruits to the BDB. You still get plenty of the original characters and of course a new love storyline. So it’s like having your cake and eating it twice!<br/><br/>Most of the book is about Paradise and Craeg, but</span>
  <span id="freeText14385956987733579461" style="display:none"><b>5 Recruit me Stars</b><br><br>I love JR WARD and I love the Black Dagger Brotherhood (BDB) series. Blood Kiss is a spin-off from the BDB series. You do not need to read the BDB books, however you get the full effect if you do. Blood Kiss is part of the Black Dagger Legacy. These books will focus on the new recruits to the BDB. You still get plenty of the original characters and of course a new love storyline. So it’s like having your cake and eating it twice!<br><br>Most of the book is about Paradise and Craeg, but just like JR WARD fashion she writes heavily on secondary characters and a huge chunk of the book is focused on Butch and Marissa. Again, I totally loved this.<br><br>Paradise is an aristocrat, but she’s not the typical one. She doesn’t want to simply keep house clean and make babies, no, she wants to fight, protect and serve. She recruits into the BDB training program and lands a coveted spot.<br><br>Craeg is a commoner, he has no title or status, but a chip on his shoulder. He’s strong and has the presence to be a leader. He makes it into the BDB training program and out of the two females that made it into the group he only has eyes for Paradise.<br><br>I gobbled this book up like mad. I couldn’t put it down and I read it in one sitting. JR WARD has a way in sucking you into these fantastic worlds. Like I said, I love the BDB books and Blood Kiss held up to any expectations I had. Blood Kiss felt like it got back to the original BDB roots, where everything is fresh and the drama is there, but at a minimal.<br><br>I adore Paradise. I love how strong, independent and strong-minded she was. I loved that even though she’s very rich and she could have any guy she wanted, she had a crush on Craeg. I couldn’t get enough of Craeg, he’s charming, and a mean guy and the Hero you want to punch and suck faces with at the same time. He doesn’t want anything to do with Paradise because he doesn’t do relationships. He’s on a mission and nothing is going to stop him, but Paradise’s kindness and persistence is hard to say no to.<br><br>Paradise and Craeg’s attraction towards each other was off the charts hot. My favorite thing about JR WARD books is all the tension she creates! I was salivating as I was reading. I enjoyed the explosive chemistry they had.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Do you like playing with fire girl? … Because if you keep looking at me like that, I’m going to burn you to the ground”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>During all of this Butch and Marissa face some relationship obstacles and it doesn’t drive a wedge between the two, but it definitely creates friction and yummy story-line. I love that JR WARD continued the couple’s story and it made the relationship in my eyes more real. Butch still has issues in never feeling good enough for Marissa and Marissa deals with Butch sometimes irrational behavior.<br><br>Overall, this book was delicious. I am completely 100% satisfied and it just makes me want to reread the BDB series again.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/9nhlUkK" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449064103i/17229642.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>An ARC was provided</i><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24903031.Blood_Kiss__Black_Dagger_Legacy___1_" title="Blood Kiss (Black Dagger Legacy, #1) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1426697749s/24903031.jpg" alt="Blood Kiss (Black Dagger Legacy, #1) by J.R. Ward" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> Blood Kiss - &gt; <a href="http://amzn.to/20fU19x" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="14385956987733579461" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1470497852" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1470497852" />
    <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish"><img alt="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1398981306p2/1113032.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1470497852?book_show_action=true">Dec 16, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="user" itemprop="url" name="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish">UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25144725-blood-kiss">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=own-have-read">own-have-read</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=author-jr-ward-jessica-bird">author-jr-ward-jessica-bird</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=4-stars">4-stars</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=series-spinoff">series-spinoff</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1470497852" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10715354469816764560"><b>3.5 stars</b><br/><br/>For years now it’s seemed that the WARDen (J.R. Ward) has been taking the Brotherhood down a different path, a path I found myself less and less inclined to follow. The stories became more Urban Fantasy than Paranormal Romance and, as became painfully clear in <i>The Shadows</i>, the WARDen’s idea of true love and <i>happily ever afters</i> was morphing into something I wanted no part of. But being a loyal fan and unwilling - or unable - to give up, it was with some trepidation and a whole lot of cau</span>
  <span id="freeText10715354469816764560" style="display:none"><b>3.5 stars</b><br /><br />For years now it’s seemed that the WARDen (J.R. Ward) has been taking the Brotherhood down a different path, a path I found myself less and less inclined to follow. The stories became more Urban Fantasy than Paranormal Romance and, as became painfully clear in <i>The Shadows</i>, the WARDen’s idea of true love and <i>happily ever afters</i> was morphing into something I wanted no part of. But being a loyal fan and unwilling - or unable - to give up, it was with some trepidation and a whole lot of cautious optimism that I began reading <i>Blood Kiss</i> because, after the debacle that was <i>The Shadows</i>, I wasn’t sure I’d ever enjoy a <i>Black Dagger Brotherhood</i> novel again. I didn’t preorder, I didn’t read reviews, I didn’t chat it up with fellow BDB lovers…I avoided any and all discussion as much as possible. Until, that is, I peeked at my Goodreads’ friends comments (thanks, Beanbag and Lenore) and decided to bite the bullet and give it a chance.<br /><br />I’m so glad I did!<br /><br />Perhaps because <i>Blood Kiss</i> is the first in the new <i>Black Dagger Legacy</i> spin-off series The WARDen was able to return us to the Brotherhood we all came to know and love way-back-when. Maybe she finally quit the Rice Krispies and went with a higher fiber cereal… who’s to say. Whatever the reason, I’m thrilled to be able to say that I really enjoyed this story and page after page saw shades of the <i>Black Dagger Brotherhood</i> that I love and have missed over the past several books. There were moments that felt New Adult-esque, and at other moments I thought the writing was simplistic, but the truth is, it’s not the writing that's simple, it's that this story isn’t complicated and all over the place. We’re back to a single couple<i> happily ever after</i>, while also spending quality time with Butch and Marissa, and Vishous.. The other Brothers and their <i>shellans</i> made appearances, too, and I loved that!<br /><br />The bottom line? <i>Blood Kiss</i> isn't perfect but it's an entertaining story and a solid start to the series. If things continue on this way, I think fans of the original books will enjoy the <i>Black Dagger Legacy</i>! </span>
  <a data-text-id="10715354469816764560" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1435375262" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1435375262" />
    <a title="Mandi Schreiner" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2704703-mandi-schreiner"><img alt="Mandi Schreiner" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1368979996p2/2704703.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1435375262?book_show_action=true">Nov 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mandi Schreiner" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mandi Schreiner" href="/user/show/2704703-mandi-schreiner">Mandi Schreiner</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2704703-mandi-schreiner?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1435375262" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6110407497379212953">First - spoiler alert! The heroine actually lives in this book. After The Shadows, you never know. (I'm still bitter - I can't help it. But I really liked this book so I'm moving on.)<br/><br/>Blood Kiss is the first spin-off book of Ward's Black Dagger Brotherhood book. It's 100% set in the BDB world, in the training center and lots of brothers and their shellans are in the book. But unlike some of the recent BDB books, this one has two main focuses - Butch/Marissa and Paradise/Craeg. As the fight agains</span>
  <span id="freeText6110407497379212953" style="display:none">First - spoiler alert! The heroine actually lives in this book. After The Shadows, you never know. (I'm still bitter - I can't help it. But I really liked this book so I'm moving on.)<br /><br />Blood Kiss is the first spin-off book of Ward's Black Dagger Brotherhood book. It's 100% set in the BDB world, in the training center and lots of brothers and their shellans are in the book. But unlike some of the recent BDB books, this one has two main focuses - Butch/Marissa and Paradise/Craeg. As the fight against the lessers increases and after that horrible massacre, the Brothers have decided to bring in some new recruits. Sixty applicants apply but after a night of intense hazing, seven remain standing. Paradise is one of two girl trainees and the one that stays on her feet the longest during the first night. I don't always love JR Ward heroines, but I enjoyed Paradise. She comes from an aristocratic family - her father is an advisor to Wrath, so it is expected for her to grow up, marry, and be the perfect hostess. But she doesn't want that. When most of her family dies during the raids, she decides she wants to train to fight. Her father reluctantly agrees, but is a good support for her throughout the book.<br /><br />Craeg is another trainee. His father was killed during the raids and he has a grudge against the aristocrats. He is grumbly and growly and tough. Craeg and Paradise have a pretty immediate connection, but he wants nothing to do with a relationship. He wants to learn to fight and that's about it. We meet the other trainees as well, as I assume all will get books. I like them all - Novo is the other female, and she reminds me a bit of Xhex. Axe is a goth/scary mofo who intrigues me. Peyton is Paradise's best friend - annoying but likable too.<br /><br />What I like best about this training center scenario is that it allows us to have fresh characters yet still have the brothers play a big role - but nothing is too muddled. Rhage, V, Butch all have pretty big roles in this book, as they put the trainees through their courses. They have to act all menacing and tough to intimate the green recruits - and it's fun. They are there eating dinner with their mates, or just passing through. It felt very warm and family-like. Lassiter is in the book a lot being....Lassiter. At one point he uses a selfie-stick to make a semi-naked calendar of just him. What I love about the BDB - the goofiness, the brotherly camaraderie, the bad-ass, sarcastic, leather-wearing men who are all gooey with their mates - it's all here. This made me very happy.<br /><br />While 50% of the book is Craeg and Paradise, the other half is Butch and Marissa. Don't worry - nothing major goes down with these two. Butch acts like a typical Brother by putting Marissa on a constant pedestal. All Marissa wants to do is be a little more dirty...not as prim and proper and Butch won't hear of it. But they talk it out through the book and work out their differences. There are some very sexy scenes with them. I adore Butch, so I'm really glad we get a "part two" to his HEA, and also that it's nothing horrible or stressful.<br /><br />The other part of the story is an unnamed victim of abuse who dies and Marissa is determined to find out who the girl is and what happened to her. Butch helps out with this mystery. It worked well within the story.<br /><br />My only complaint about the story is that the "I love you" between Paradise and Craeg felt rushed and forced to me. I definitely felt their chemistry and I like how their relationship was progressing, but it felt no where near the I love you stage. I really feel they barely get to know each other in this book. Craeg has that bonding scent released and his fangs out anytime anyone gets near Paradise, but it felt rushed to me.<br /><br />Otherwise, Blood Kiss is a fun book. It has that BDB humor I enjoy and lots of sexy times. Blood Kiss reminds me why I love spending time with the brothers.<br /><br />Grade: B</span>
  <a data-text-id="6110407497379212953" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1447650073" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1447650073" />
    <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel"><img alt="♥Rachel♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1363996055p2/5481477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1447650073?book_show_action=true">Nov 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥Rachel♥" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel">♥Rachel♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5481477-rachel?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5481477-rachel?shelf=mystery">mystery</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1447650073" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14511447306066697825"><b><br/>Blood Kiss </b>was an exciting start to J.R.Ward’s new spinoff series, Black Dagger Legacy, and we still get our favorite Black Dagger Brothers, as well! <br/><br/>Paradise, the blooded daughter of the advisor to the King would like to break free of the restrictive life she’s used to. As a daughter of privilege and wealth she’s expected to mate with someone from her own class and have children, but Paradise has other plans. Enrolling in the Brother’s Warrior academy she wants to train to protect her people fr</span>
  <span id="freeText14511447306066697825" style="display:none"><b><br />Blood Kiss </b>was an exciting start to J.R.Ward’s new spinoff series, Black Dagger Legacy, and we still get our favorite Black Dagger Brothers, as well! <br /><br />Paradise, the blooded daughter of the advisor to the King would like to break free of the restrictive life she’s used to. As a daughter of privilege and wealth she’s expected to mate with someone from her own class and have children, but Paradise has other plans. Enrolling in the Brother’s Warrior academy she wants to train to protect her people from the Lessers and any other threats. The training is physically and mentally challenging, but Paradise is determined to succeed and excel. She hadn’t planned on finding love, but she can’t keep her mind and body from straying to one of her teammates, Craeg. <br /><br />Craeg has enrolled in Warrior’s Academy to train and avenge his father’s murder. His gorgeous teammate, Paradise, is a distraction he doesn’t need or want. Craeg struggles with the overwhelming pull she has on him and his protective and possessive instincts come raging to life anytime Paradise is around. <br /><br />Butch and Marissa love each other, but their relationship is put to the test when a girl is brutally assaulted and ends up at Safe Place, in Marissa’s care. <br /><br />I was immediately sucked into both of these stories, because really this is two stories unfolding at once: Craeg and Paradise’s trials and romance as they try to survive the academy training and Butch and Marissa’s <s>marriage</s> mating in crisis. Both stories were compelling in their own way. Craeg and Paradise are the younger set. You could put them in the New Adult age range, so I guess J.R. Ward sort of wrote her way into that category with <b>Blood Kiss</b>, but thankfully that’s where all similarities with NA end. No unnecessary drama or angst; just two people trying to succeed under pressure, all the while fighting a deliciously intense attraction. Such a wonderful build of sexual tension! They had some roadblocks to navigate; a mystery filled with danger, as well. <br /><br />I felt Butch and Marissa’s story acutely, because there is never a HEA that you don’t have to work at and every relationship must grow and overcome obstacles. I enjoyed watching Butch and Marissa work through issues, with all the messy emotions, and come to a deeper level of understanding and connection, because these two really do love each other!<br /><br />In the past, with the <b>Black Dagger Brotherhood</b> series, I’ve struggled to read the Lesser’s chapters, mostly I just skimmed through them. So I was thrilled there was no Lesser POV in <b>Blood Kiss</b>! <br /><br />J.R. Ward’s world of vampire warriors with its rules of feeding, bonding, mating and hierarchy is riveting! She made a fantasy come to life with real world emotions and trials that anyone could relate to. I think <b>Blood Kiss</b> will be a thrilling, fresh exploration of the Black Dagger world for established fans, and an enticing start for any new readers. <br /> <i><br />A copy was kindly provided by Signet in exchange for an honest review.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="14511447306066697825" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">
          

<tr class="no_border feedFooterReview" id="update_comment_stuff_Review1447650073">

<div id="review_1196707887" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1196707887" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1088245-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1359727841p2/1088245.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1196707887?book_show_action=true">Feb 10, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/1088245-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1088245-debra?shelf=part-of-series-or-serial">part-of-series-or-serial</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1088245-debra?shelf=library-book">library-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1088245-debra?shelf=paranormal-vampires">paranormal-vampires</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1196707887" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8441627081597606733"><b>I'm torn between 3 and 3.5 so maybe 3.25 I liked but didn't love it stars?</b><br/><br/>After being pleasantly surprised by The Shadows I decided to go for this one. I really have missed the focus on the "original" brothers and was glad to get some more face time with them. It was all of the domestic variety rather than the slaying variety, but that was fine by me. This will probably be less of a review and more of a like/dislike. <br/><br/>The part of the story focusing on the trainees had a very New Adult feel and th</span>
  <span id="freeText8441627081597606733" style="display:none"><b>I'm torn between 3 and 3.5 so maybe 3.25 I liked but didn't love it stars?</b><br /><br />After being pleasantly surprised by The Shadows I decided to go for this one. I really have missed the focus on the "original" brothers and was glad to get some more face time with them. It was all of the domestic variety rather than the slaying variety, but that was fine by me. This will probably be less of a review and more of a like/dislike. <br /><br />The part of the story focusing on the trainees had a very New Adult feel and the beginning of the book took me forever to get through for some reason. I liked it but didn't love it. I liked all the new recruits enough and would like to get to know them more. Paradise and Craeg worked more for me as friends and teammates. The are both strong and would be great co-leaders of the team. Sadly, I just didn't feel the chemistry between them (to me she had more chemistry with Peyton). I do like that both Paradise and Novo are strong, independent women doing more than just holding their own with the guys. I loved the way Butch related to Craeg and Axe. He is the perfect mentor for these two men and I hope the next books will continue with that relationship.<br /><br />Butch, V and Marissa get lots of time in this one. Marissa has really come into herself as a character. Her bonding time with V was something I was glad to see since he is so intertwined with Butch. Their issues weren't earth shattering, but normal long-term couple needing to reboot and communicate better. I would have liked to see more resolution of her relationship with Havers and I would really love to see Butch working toward establishing a police force. It was also nice to see all the females spend some time and bond and be supportive of each other. <br /><br />Finally, we have Lassiter! Can we please find Lassiter a man. I love it every time he is on the page. Put him together with Axe or, even better yet, he could probably do wonders for Saxton - that would surely get the glymera's tongues wagging! <br /><br />Overall it was a good but not great story, a lot more focused than the last few BDB books with the 1001 storylines, but enough potential to keep me reading the next one.<br /><br /><br /><br /><b>Pre-release thoughts: After The King I knew I was pretty much done with the BDB. The Shadows isn't even on my TBR at the moment. If this really is everything I loved about the series in the early days without everything I've come to loathe about the latest few books I will be a very happy girl. </b></span>
  <a data-text-id="8441627081597606733" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1250154373" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1250154373" />
    <a title="Auntee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/886675-auntee"><img alt="Auntee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1281897695p2/886675.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1250154373?book_show_action=true">Apr 09, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Auntee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Auntee" href="/user/show/886675-auntee">Auntee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of the BDB.  Paranormal romance fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=2015_reads">2015_reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1250154373" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8254539635010258046">I think I waited a bit too long to review this since I feel like I lost <i>some</i> of the feeling I had for the book after I finished...but I'm going to try and get it back.<br/><br/>I know I enjoyed it<i> a lot</i>. I liked the set up of having the Brothers starting a training program for recruits in the fight against the Lessers. There's lots of potential here, and after the first arduous training class (that was the physical/suspenseful highlight of the book) we're left with just seven recruits. So surely there'll </span>
  <span id="freeText8254539635010258046" style="display:none">I think I waited a bit too long to review this since I feel like I lost <i>some</i> of the feeling I had for the book after I finished...but I'm going to try and get it back.<br><br>I know I enjoyed it<i> a lot</i>. I liked the set up of having the Brothers starting a training program for recruits in the fight against the Lessers. There's lots of potential here, and after the first arduous training class (that was the physical/suspenseful highlight of the book) we're left with just seven recruits. So surely there'll be more classes and we'll have the potential to read about even more characters, because this battle against the Lessers is going to be a long one...<br><br>The book focuses on two couples. Our new 'couple', the 'uptown' aristocratic 'good girl' Paradise and her 'downtown guy', commoner Craeg. They get to share the pages with old favorites, 'downtown' Butch and 'uptown' 'good girl' Marissa. Interesting how the author focused on two couples with similar backgrounds...<br><br> Butch and Marissa have hit a bump in their marriage, and we get some insight about why Butch has her high upon that pedestal, and wonder if Marissa will<i> ever</i> get to come off it.<br><br>I liked reading about Butch and Marissa, problems and all. I remembered<i> loving</i> Butch's book (and had a great desire to go back and reread his story!) and it was nice to revisit these characters. I never had any doubt that they could work things out, so their plot wasn't all that suspenseful. They did have some pretty <i>hot</i> moments, and I liked seeing Butch open up to Marissa and treat her like a true <i>partner</i>, rather than like someone he has to constantly protect. By the end of the book I felt they were solid as a couple, and would continue to share everything with each other.<br><br><i>Craeg</i>...<br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/aunteecr002/reviews/8107428c-f44d-4ffa-8445-2aa21d6fe64e_zpslsemifxq.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450501826i/17436671.jpg" alt=" photo 8107428c-f44d-4ffa-8445-2aa21d6fe64e_zpslsemifxq.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Paradise...</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/aunteecr002/reviews/35906be5-a0e1-401e-9eb7-cec55489b2ce_zpsq0daedfr.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450502089i/17436722.jpg" alt=" photo 35906be5-a0e1-401e-9eb7-cec55489b2ce_zpsq0daedfr.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I liked reading about Paradise and Craeg as well. It's harder to feel the same connection to them because we don't know as much about them--they haven't really been featured in books like Butch -and to a lesser extent, Marissa- were before they got their own book, so we have to get to know them--fast. And while Ward does a pretty good job at giving them both an adequate back story, it's hard, really hard, not to compare them to the other main couple in the book. I did like their chemistry, but I felt that <i>maybe</i> the ILYs came a wee bit too fast? I thought maybe their story arc would carry over to the next book, or maybe their ILYs would, if that makes sense. I guess I'm used to those big long BDB books, and not used to Ward writing a tight, concise romance!<br><br>But for the first in a (spin-off) series? Very well done. I see some potential in new recruits Peyton, Novo, Axe, and Boone and look forward to their stories. Same Ward writing style, same touches of humor (Lassiter had me lol more than a few times!), and seeing (and hearing) most of the Brothers? (But especially Butch and V?) That's enough to tide me over until March and <b>The Beast</b>.<br><br>4 1/2 stars</span>
  <a data-text-id="8254539635010258046" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1416825871" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1416825871" />
    <a title="Sophia Triad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad"><img alt="Sophia Triad" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591419108p2/44642860.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1416825871?book_show_action=true">Oct 14, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Triad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Triad" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad">Sophia Triad</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=1paranormal-lovestories">1paranormal-lovestories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=fangywarriorteams">fangywarriorteams</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1416825871" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13964698584990175815"><b>Paradise and Craeg</b><br/><br/>Here comes the next generation! New kids in town…<br/>The training centre is open again and all the vampires are welcome.<br/>There is no discrimination, if a vampire wants to join. <br/>Females and Males are welcome. Lowly vampires as well as arrogant glymera royalties are welcome. <br/>Everyone can become the next warrior against the lesser.<br/>Everyone can become the next Brother.<br/>As long as they are willing to be beaten to death, to almost die, to almost drown, to be humiliated, to walk until they </span>
  <span id="freeText13964698584990175815" style="display:none"><b>Paradise and Craeg</b><br /><br />Here comes the next generation! New kids in town…<br />The training centre is open again and all the vampires are welcome.<br />There is no discrimination, if a vampire wants to join. <br />Females and Males are welcome. Lowly vampires as well as arrogant glymera royalties are welcome. <br />Everyone can become the next warrior against the lesser.<br />Everyone can become the next Brother.<br />As long as they are willing to be beaten to death, to almost die, to almost drown, to be humiliated, to walk until they fall on their face, to push every limit they have. And all these will happen to them, before even they start training.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Doesn’t mean I’m happy about introducing a bunch of children into the war.”<br />“We either make the intros, or the war will find them on its own terms.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />So, everyone will be here to test their limitations. <br />Peyton, Axe, Boone, Novo, Anslam, Paradise and so many others…<br />But where is Craeg?<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>The sound of a door closing made her glance over her shoulder—and she gasped before she could help herself.<br />There he was, the one she had waited for, the one she had hoped to see again.<br />Paradise patted at her ponytail, some estrogen-linked receptor going bat-shit, sixteen-year-old as the male walked over to the sign-in station.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />Paradise wants Craeg.<br />Peyton wants Paradise.<br />Craeg wants to finish the training program because this is the only future he can have.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“You can’t do both?”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />Obviously Craeg’s iron will won’t last long. I absolutely loved their first time together. It was sloppy, without thinking and they behaved exactly like two horny 20something kids in love should behave.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Are you sure?” he mumbled. While he started undoing the front of his jeans.<br />“Do you want me to beg?”<br />“No, because I’d start coming right now.”<br />He glanced around and didn’t see any cameras. But that didn’t mean the fuckers weren’t somewhere hidden. “I wish there was another place we could do this.”<br />“Like I care where we are.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />Overall, I absolutely loved glymera sweetheart Paradise and poor but honorable Craeg together!<br />I am so happy that Ward has added so many young and interesting characters and this new spinoff is definitely a success.<br /><br />P.S. The book also includes an update on Butch and Marissa’s life as a couple. Always nice to meet again the main characters from BDB.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13964698584990175815" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=review-requests">review-requests</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-i-go-rabid-over">books-i-go-rabid-over</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=for-fresh-fiction-review">for-fresh-fiction-review</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1201554358" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8321765905681167515"><a href='http://www.underthecoversbookblog.com/2015/12/blood-kiss-by-j-r-ward.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430489640i/14717740.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> <br/><br/>What were your first thoughts when you learned that Ward was going to be returning to the training centre and giving us stories about new trainees?<br/><br/>Annie: I was excited! J.R. Ward is my all-time favorite author and I knew that going back to the training centre would give readers an intimate and in depth look into how the Brotherhood worked. And although Ward essentially went back to basics, it was the most natural course to take in this series with the brewing war with the Lessers.<br/><br/>These new </span>
  <span id="freeText8321765905681167515" style="display:none"><a href="http://www.underthecoversbookblog.com/2015/12/blood-kiss-by-j-r-ward.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430489640i/14717740.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>What were your first thoughts when you learned that Ward was going to be returning to the training centre and giving us stories about new trainees?<br><br>Annie: I was excited! J.R. Ward is my all-time favorite author and I knew that going back to the training centre would give readers an intimate and in depth look into how the Brotherhood worked. And although Ward essentially went back to basics, it was the most natural course to take in this series with the brewing war with the Lessers.<br><br>These new recruits all have their own set of experiences that have molded and defined them and they bring that to the program every time they train. I have my favorites already and can’t wait to see what Ward has planned for them next!<br><br>Francesca: So excited! My favorite moments in this series go back to the training center with JM, Blay and Qhuinn and being able to revisit that while seeing some of my favorite brothers as the head of the program was like a dream! I think although she’s going back to the concept, she’s doing it in a fresh new way as this training center is nothing like it was then. We are not dealing with inexperienced pre-trans here and it was a lot of fun to see. I think fans will be very pleased.<br><br>What did you think of the other trainees? (Anslam, Peyton, Novo, Axe and Boone)<br><br>Annie:<br><br>Anslam: Ugh.<br><br>Peyton: He can be a jerk but a guy’s guy kind of character, the one that doesn’t like to admit he likes something unless it’s cool to do so. But I have a feeling that Ward will bring him to his knees :)<br><br>Novo: Love her! She reminds me a lot of Xhex so I’m wondering if in her book if we will see more of Xhex and JM.<br><br>Axe: This guy also reminds me of one of the Brothers, V. There’s no doubt that the two of these guys would get along well. I can only hope that we’ll revisit more of V and his kinky side.<br><br>Boone: This guy is an easy one to forget but I am not fooled for a minute that Ward doesn’t have something up her sleeve with this character.<br><br>Francesca:<br><br>I don’t want to give too much away but I can already see how some of them mold after other characters we already love. I especially loved Novo because she’s the other female to make it into the training program and she’s very much like Xhex. I have hopes for a romance between her and another one of the recruits… <br><br>The rest of the guys are quite like the current BDB. There’s a kinky one, a buff one and a couple of pretty boys. But I KNOW with Ward things are not always what they seem and I can’t wait to explore more of them all.<br><br>Which of them are you most excited about?<br><br>Annie: Definitely Novo and Axe. Novo seems like a tough as nails character from what we have seen of her so far, but she also has that playful side as well that is open to anything. I can’t wait to see what Ward has in store for her.<br><br>Axe is probably the one I’m most intrigued about. Ward dipped into his backstory a little bit but I’m dying for more. Who would’ve thought that a kinky Goth would excite me?<br><br>Francesca: Like I said before, I’m most excited about Novo. We know from first impressions she’s tough and can hang with the boys easily but as the book progresses she lets us in to her softer side, even as a romantic with her matchmaking skills. I can’t wait to delve deeper into her character and see how she will bring her male to heel. <br><br>What did you think of Paradise and Craeg? Did you like their romance?<br><br>Annie: They were a great pair. Ward builds their romance in a believable manner and this is something to note because one, these characters are younger so they are a little more hesitant with conveying their emotions and two, IT’S NOT INSTALOVE! After all the books that seem to jump into love so quickly, I love that Craeg has his reservations about Paradise. He thinks she’s too good for him and there are a bunch of reverent lines that absolutely melted my heart. I also liked that Paradise had no problem telling him off when he was being too stubborn.<br><br>Francesca: I think they were so adorable. Great first pairing in this new “series”. Their romance is a constant presence throughout the story even when it takes a while for them to get together. I liked that slow pacing, although I would’ve preferred a little bit more of meat between when they first got together and their I love yous. Craeg is just the best. He’s determined and a fighter. In everything he sets his mind to. I loved him! And I think Paradise is one of Ward’s best heroines from the start. She’s got balls and smarts. She goes after the male she wants and she won’t let anyone push her around, not even him. You can definitely tell they are younger characters but that didn’t take anything away from the way they perfectly fit with the Brotherhood.<br><br>Alongside Paradise and Craeg, Butch and Marissa are the other main couple featured in BLOOD KISS. What did you think about their storyline?<br><br>Annie: For me, it was natural to see Marissa and Butch sharing the page time with Paradise and Craeg because their stories aren’t that different from one another. The females are born into a world filled with position and power but because of their sex, they are boxed in with expectations and traditions, preventing them from making their own decisions about their own life. Craeg is very much like Butch too. He’s from a different world than the one Paradise was raised in. He knows that and yet he can’t seem to resist her.<br><br>When Ward said she was revisiting some of the past couples we’ve come to love, I was a little worried about what might happen. I was glad that Ward didn’t break them down only to put them back together. But as with any relationship there are rough patches and that is what Ward explores here. Some distance is created but it isn’t something that can’t be dealt with with some communication. In this type of situation, I was happy for the swift resolution. It’s not to the point where the author is milking everything from her characters just to produce a book. Butch and Marissa’s storyline is the perfect compliment to Paradise and Craeg’s main dish.<br><br>Francesca: I completely agree with Annie, they were the natural choice to place in this book. I was more than a little giddy to see Butch heading the training program and in doing so, we had to revisit with him on a more personal front. Marissa has always seemed one of the weaker heroines in the series, with her coming from the glymera and being pushed aside by Wrath for so long. I needed to see her find her stronger self and Ward did an amazing job at that in this book. I may have wanted to throttle Butch a time or two but good for Marissa for showing the male how things should be done and handled. This resolved some long pushed down unfinished business and it only makes the series stronger to see that side of their relationships. Perfect!<br><br>Do you have a favourite scene in the book?<br><br>Annie: Oh, it has to be the Magic Mike XXL scenes. I literally laughed my ass off while reading those parts. Of course Ward had to put her man, Channing in her book, right? It was nice to see all the girls together, just having a good time. Doesn’t hurt to see the men sulking either, does it.<br><br>All in all, BLOOD KISS exceeded my expectations. Once again, J.R. Ward shows the world how Paranormal Romance is done!<br><br>Francesca: I know this is so not about the main couple of anything but I have to say Lassiter and his calendar. The jokes about the selfie stick and Kinkos just about did me in. I absolutely love him, can I keep him?<br><br>BLOOD KISS is very much another book in the Black Dagger Brotherhood. It didn’t feel like a separate series, which I was worried about. Ward knows how to give fans exactly what they crave and this hit that mark for all of us long time fans of the series. Giving us everything we loved from before mixed in with enough of what we love now. Still to date, the best paranormal romance author out there.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8321765905681167515" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1456611109" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1456611109" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6049062-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460575899p2/6049062.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1456611109?book_show_action=true">Dec 01, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=series-book">series-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=paranormal-supernatural">paranormal-supernatural</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=december-2015">december-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1456611109" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9111071086169393874">Oh...MY....GOODNESS!!!! This book has had me so darn excited!!!! And I have to admit that it has been far too long since I have enjoyed a book quite this much! Also, far too long since I have felt that passion I use to when I first started reading the BDB series!! In my opinion, this new "spin-off" series is classic JR Ward. You know, back when the BDB books were, sexy and exciting, and let us not forget....so damn funny! In this particular book there is a scene that had me literally laughing ou</span>
  <span id="freeText9111071086169393874" style="display:none">Oh...MY....GOODNESS!!!! This book has had me so darn excited!!!! And I have to admit that it has been far too long since I have enjoyed a book quite this much! Also, far too long since I have felt that passion I use to when I first started reading the BDB series!! In my opinion, this new "spin-off" series is classic JR Ward. You know, back when the BDB books were, sexy and exciting, and let us not forget....so damn funny! In this particular book there is a scene that had me literally laughing out loud so hard that I disturbed my hubby's tv watching!!! LOL I think he began to think I was crazy!!!<br />Let us just say that the scene consisted of a girl's night for the mated women.....and what were they doing???? Well, watching "Magic Mike" of course!!! Remember that bonded vampire males are extremely possessive of their females....LMAO!!! You get the idea...The one liners, and everything that transpired was amazingly entertaining and I won't ever forget it!<br /><br />I kind of got off track! This series is about a younger generation of vamps that are participating in a training centre program run by our favorite Brothers. Out of hundreds of candidates, only seven make it through, and these seven will train to fight in the war that has developed after the tragic raids that happened in the BDB world.<br /><br />In this installment we watch Paradise, who is the daughter of Abalone fall in love with a "commoner" vampire named Craeg. They are both recruits at the training centre and they have an intense attraction to one another. Woven in between their romance is a closer look into the relationship of Butch and Marissa. I found these two couples to be a perfect fit for this book as we have both men who are considered from a "lower class" than their females. The parallel between Butch/Craeg and Marissa/Paradise is a genius move on JR Ward's part and she couldn't have done it better in my opinion.<br /><br />So, not only do we get the treat of meeting exciting new characters; but we are given a glimpse into our beloved BDB characters who I feel like I have known for years!<br />I LOVED it! I loved every part of it, and the only thing I really grumbled about was it ending! This book has reminded me of why I love to read! It also reminded me that when you have a very talented author writing a story, I become transported into the story as if I'm right there beside the characters. I have honestly missed that in my reading for quite some time. It doesn't mean that I haven't read some good books, it just means that there are a very few that literally captivate me like "Blood Kiss" did.<br /><br />Were there some flaws??? Maybe just a few. I would have loved more page time between Craeg and Paradise...He had his walls up pretty high for a big portion of the book, and it would have been nice to see him fight his attraction to paradise just a little bit less. The thing is though, I was so enjoying Butch and Marissa's page time too...so all in all I won't complain too much!<br /><br />This is a MUST read for BDB lovers. For the readers that have left the series because it was getting way too confusing and complex....Give this one a try! I think you will be won back, as this is a reminder of why we fell in love with the Brotherhood in the beginning! This book will remind you of the magic we all experienced way back with Wrath and Beth!!<br /><br />I can't wait to see which trainee is next! I am going to sit and enjoy my renewed excitement for my BDB family!!! </span>
  <a data-text-id="9111071086169393874" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1944141622" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1944141622" />
    <a title="warhawke" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25494927-warhawke"><img alt="warhawke" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1431835527p2/25494927.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1944141622?book_show_action=true">Mar 17, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="warhawke" class="user" itemprop="url" name="warhawke" href="/user/show/25494927-warhawke">warhawke</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Vamps lovers</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=romance-love">romance-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=paranormal-sci-fi-fantasy">paranormal-sci-fi-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1944141622" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16048539055678744990"><b>Genre: </b>Paranormal/Urban Fantasy<br/><b>Type: </b>Book 1 of Black Dagger Legacy series<br/><b>POV: </b>Third Person <br/><b>Rating: </b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454075031i/17913446.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1489924612i/22262634.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>As a daughter of the Founding Family, Paradise was brought up in a gilded cage. She was expected to be prim and proper, and adhere to the aristocratic standard. Desperate to break free, she decided to do the complete opposite by joining the Black Dagger Brotherhood training.<br/><br/>Craeg lost everything during the tragic period of their race. With a single focus on mind, he joined the training to prove his</span>
  <span id="freeText16048539055678744990" style="display:none"><b>Genre: </b>Paranormal/Urban Fantasy<br><b>Type: </b>Book 1 of Black Dagger Legacy series<br><b>POV: </b>Third Person <br><b>Rating: </b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454075031i/17913446.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1489924612i/22262634.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As a daughter of the Founding Family, Paradise was brought up in a gilded cage. She was expected to be prim and proper, and adhere to the aristocratic standard. Desperate to break free, she decided to do the complete opposite by joining the Black Dagger Brotherhood training.<br><br>Craeg lost everything during the tragic period of their race. With a single focus on mind, he joined the training to prove his worth and the last thing he needed was a distraction from his goal.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453882133i/17883711.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I still have catching up to do with the BDB, but I can't help by being curious of this series, so here I am lol!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>“Do you like playing with fire, girl?” he growled. “Because if you keep looking at me like that, I’m going to burn you to the ground.”</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>I love Craeg. He had that typical brooding male persona that appeal to me. He was also an alpha without having too much of the "in your face" attitude.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1489923897i/22262522.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Though I don't like the name Paradise (lol!), I do like her as a character. I like how she fought for her independence and wasn't afraid to put her foot down.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>“You have never had to worry about where your next meal is coming from, you live in a fucking museum showcase of beautiful things—and pardon me, but you don’t know what it’s like to have people look down on you because you lost the DNA lottery!”</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>One notable difference in this book compared to the BDB series is that the storyline was much simpler. Instead of a wider story with the happenings in their world, it focused more on the main characters' relationship, with the original BDB couple Butch and Marissa as the secondary couple.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>"I literally have nothing waiting for me. So I won’t let anything or anyone get in my way.”</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>The underlying matter in this book was the differences of social status between both couples. I like seeing how each of them handled the issue.<br><br>Blood Kiss is the first book in the Black Dagger Legacy series. Looking forward to get to know all the new characters and be reacquainted with the old BDB favorites.<br><br><i><b>Note 1: </b><br>Axe is my favorite but I need to catch up with the original series before reading it :(<br><br><b>Note 2:</b><br>Lassiter is probably the most lovable annoying character haha!</i><br><br><br><b>Books in the series:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24903031.Blood_Kiss__Black_Dagger_Legacy___1_" title="Blood Kiss (Black Dagger Legacy, #1) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1426697749s/24903031.jpg" alt="Blood Kiss (Black Dagger Legacy, #1) by J.R. Ward" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29496208.Blood_Vow__Black_Dagger_Legacy___2_" title="Blood Vow (Black Dagger Legacy, #2) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1461428631s/29496208.jpg" alt="Blood Vow (Black Dagger Legacy, #2) by J.R. Ward" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/34019141.Blood_Fury__Black_Dagger_Legacy___3_" title="Blood Fury (Black Dagger Legacy, #3) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">
